## Design System

### Color Palette
```css
/* Primary Colors */
--primary-blue: #1976d2;
--primary-dark: #115293;
--primary-light: #42a5f5;

/* Secondary Colors */
--secondary-orange: #ff9800;
--secondary-dark: #f57c00;
--secondary-light: #ffb74d;

/* Status Colors */
--success-green: #4caf50;
--warning-yellow: #ff9800;
--error-red: #f44336;
--info-blue: #2196f3;

/* Neutral Colors */
--gray-50: #fafafa;
--gray-100: #f5f5f5;
--gray-200: #eeeeee;
--gray-300: #e0e0e0;
--gray-400: #bdbdbd;
--gray-500: #9e9e9e;
--gray-600: #757575;
--gray-700: #616161;
--gray-800: #424242;
--gray-900: #212121;
```

### Typography
```css
/* Font Family */
font-family: 'Roboto', 'Helvetica', 'Arial', sans-serif;

/* Font Sizes */
--text-xs: 0.75rem;    /* 12px */
--text-sm: 0.875rem;   /* 14px */
--text-base: 1rem;     /* 16px */
--text-lg: 1.125rem;   /* 18px */
--text-xl: 1.25rem;    /* 20px */
--text-2xl: 1.5rem;    /* 24px */
--text-3xl: 1.875rem;  /* 30px */
--text-4xl: 2.25rem;   /* 36px */
```

### Layout Grid
- **Container Max Width**: 1200px
- **Grid Columns**: 12-column system
- **Breakpoints**: 
  - Mobile: 320px - 768px
  - Tablet: 768px - 1024px
  - Desktop: 1024px+

## Manufacturing Module

### Production Dashboard

## Responsive Design Notes

### Breakpoint Strategy
```css
/* Mobile First Approach */
.container {
  /* Mobile: 320px - 768px */
  padding: 1rem;
  font-size: 14px;
}

@media (min-width: 768px) {
  /* Tablet: 768px - 1024px */
  .container {
    padding: 1.5rem;
    font-size: 16px;
  }
}

@media (min-width: 1024px) {
  /* Desktop: 1024px+ */
  .container {
    padding: 2rem;
    font-size: 16px;
    max-width: 1200px;
    margin: 0 auto;
  }
}
```

### Component Adaptations
- **Navigation**: Collapsible sidebar on mobile, fixed sidebar on desktop
- **Tables**: Horizontal scroll on mobile, card layout for complex data
- **Forms**: Single column on mobile, multi-column on desktop
- **Charts**: Simplified on mobile, full-featured on desktop
- **Dashboards**: Stacked widgets on mobile, grid layout on desktop

### Accessibility Features
- **Keyboard Navigation**: Full keyboard support for all interactions
- **Screen Reader**: ARIA labels and semantic HTML structure
- **Color Contrast**: WCAG 2.1 AA compliant color combinations
- **Font Scaling**: Support for browser font size preferences
- **Focus Indicators**: Clear visual focus indicators for all interactive elements

---

This comprehensive frontend screen design covers all major modules of the Steel Manufacturing ERP system, providing a complete user experience across web and mobile platforms. The designs follow modern UI/UX principles with consistent branding, intuitive navigation, and responsive layouts suitable for manufacturing environments.
